44. Darul Ifta (Reference Only)
Info


Organization: Darul Ifta 


Location Basis: Bradford (Longitude W001 45, Latitude N53 48) 


Calculation Basis: Sehri End/Fajr is when the Sun is 18° below the eastern astronomical horizon. Iftari/Maghrib is adding five minutes to the time when the Sun is 0.83° below the astronomical horizon.
+1


Sadaqatul Fitr: Wheat (£4.00), Barley (£6.10), Khudri dates (£14.15), Safawi dates (£24.70), Medjool dates (£35.40), Raisins (£13.60) .

Timetable Data
